SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_03_FILE##4071171 COCA  A    0   46 It describes the actions , practices , and virtues constitutive of eudaimonia--happiness or flourishing within this life. n9 Thomistic virtue theory maintains this basic structure , n10 although it redefines and relocates true eudaimonia , identifying it as lasting friendship with God throughout eternity. ( n11 ) <p> Whether secular or Christian , an action theory rooted in or indebted to a virtue-centered approach to morality analyzes moral actions from in Thomistic thought , the fundamental moral description of an action is generally taken from an agent 's immediate purpose or " object " in acting. n12 The agent 's motives , as well as the circumstances of his or her action , can affect the moral quality of the action , which then affects the agent 's character .

SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_03_FILE##4071171 COCA  A    0  307 Rights theory promotes an actual state of affairs that gives each and every person his or her due in justice--as Aquinas said , justice is a virtue focused on external operations , pointing to the actual impact that our actions have on others. SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_03_FILE##4071171 COCA  A    0  319 A quasi-integral part of the virtue of prudence , the habit of understanding , shapes the correct grasp of a universal principle in a particular instance. ( n83 ) Empathetic imagination might be considered an instantiation of the habit of circumspection , another quasi-integral part of prudence that allows us properly to perceive the morally relevant circumstances of our action. ( n84 ) Finally , we might think about strategic imagination as an aspect of shrewdness , the broader contours of a particular situation rapidly and reliably , so that we can promote human rights as best we can in less-than-ideal situations. ( n85 ) <p> Those committed to human rights face some dark times at the present in both the practical and theoretical arenas : egregious abuses of human rights are all too common throughout the globe , and the very idea of human rights is under serious attack from a wide range of theoretical perspectives. ( n86 ) I hope this article has contributed in some small way to the defense of human rights by highlighting the character traits that enable their recognition and protection in concrete cases .
